<script type="text/javascript">


var analytics = (function(){

    var webType = 'desktop';
    var isInApp = false;
    var appPlatform = '';
    var piwikEnabled = false;
    var gtmId = 'GTM-5XJPTB';

    var inappAnalyticsNamespace = {
        "analyticsScreen": "analyticsScreen",
        "analyticsEvent": "analyticsEvent",
        "checkoutSuccess": "checkoutSuccess",
        "checkoutFail": "checkoutFail",
        "initiateCheckout": "initiateCheckout",
        "registerSuccess": "registerSuccess"
    };

    var piwikTrackPage = function(pageUrl){
        if (!piwikEnabled) return false;

        if(typeof window.hktvUUID != 'undefined'){
            _paq.push(['setCustomDimension', 1, window.hktvUUID.readCookie('ott-uuid')]);
        }
        if(pageUrl != "undefined" && pageUrl != null) {
            _paq.push(['trackPageView', pageUrl]);
        }
        else{_paq.push(['trackPageView']);}
        return true;
    };

    var piwikTrackEvent = function(category, action, opt_label){
        if (!piwikEnabled) return false;

        if(typeof window.hktvUUID != 'undefined'){
            _paq.push(['setCustomDimension', 1, window.hktvUUID.readCookie('ott-uuid')]);
        }
        _paq.push(['trackEvent', category, action, opt_label]);
        return true;
    };

    var piwikAddEcommerceItem = function(productSKU, productName, productCategory, price, quantity){
        if (!piwikEnabled) return false;

        _paq.push(['addEcommerceItem', productSKU, productName, productCategory, price, quantity]);
        return true;
    };

    var piwikTrackEcommerceOrder = function(orderId, grandTotal, subTotal, tax, shipping, discount){
        if (!piwikEnabled) return false;

        if(typeof window.hktvUUID != 'undefined'){
            _paq.push(['setCustomDimension', 1, window.hktvUUID.readCookie('ott-uuid')]);
        }
        _paq.push(['trackEcommerceOrder', orderId, 0]);
        return true;
    };

    // android inApp WebView tunneling tracking

    var androidTrackPage = function(pageUrl){
        if ( typeof window.nativeConversion !== "undefined" && typeof window.nativeConversion.analyticsScreen !== "undefined"){
            window.nativeConversion.analyticsScreen(pageUrl);
        }
    };
    var androidTrackEvent = function(category, action, opt_label){
        if ( typeof window.nativeConversion !== "undefined" && typeof window.nativeConversion.analyticsEvent !== "undefined"){
            window.nativeConversion.analyticsEvent(category, action, opt_label);
        }
    };

    var pushGTMDataLayer = function(data){
        if(gtmId == '') return false;

        if(typeof dataLayer !== "undefined")
            dataLayer.push(data);
        return true;
    };
    var trackGTMCustomEvent = function(eventName){
        if(gtmId == '') return false;

        if(typeof dataLayer !== "undefined")
            dataLayer.push({'event':eventName});
        return true;
    };

    var trackPage = function(pageUrl){
        if(pageUrl != "undefined" && pageUrl != null) {
            pushGTMDataLayer({'event':'hktvGAvirtualPage', 'virtualPage':pageUrl});
        }
        else {
            pushGTMDataLayer({'event':'hktvGApage'});
        }

        if (webType == 'mobile' && isInApp){
            if(pageUrl != "undefined" && pageUrl != null) {
                InappCommunicationManager.sendAnalytics(inappAnalyticsNamespace.analyticsScreen, {"name": pageUrl});
                if (appPlatform== 'android')
                    androidTrackPage(pageUrl);
            }
        }
        else {
            try {
                piwikTrackPage(pageUrl);
            }
            catch (error) {}
        }
        return true;
    };

    var trackEvent = function(category, action, opt_label, nonInteraction){
        pushGTMDataLayer({'event':'hktvGAevent', 'nonInteraction': (nonInteraction != "undefined" && nonInteraction == true?true:false), 'eventCategory':category, 'eventAction':action, 'eventLabel':opt_label});

        if (webType == 'mobile' && isInApp){
            InappCommunicationManager.sendAnalytics(inappAnalyticsNamespace.analyticsEvent, {
                "category": category,
                "action": action,
                "label": opt_label
            });
            if (appPlatform== 'android')
                androidTrackEvent(category, action, opt_label);
        }
        else{
            try{
                piwikTrackEvent(category, action, opt_label);
            }
            catch(error) {}
        }
        return true;
    };

    
    var trackEcommerceOrder = function(orderId, siteName, products){
        pushGTMDataLayer({'event':'hktvEcommerce',
          'ecommerce':{
            'purchase': {
              'actionField': {
                'id': orderId,
                'affiliation': siteName,
                'revenue': '0',
                'tax':'0',
                'shipping': '0',
                'coupon': ''
              },
              'products': products
            }
          }
        });

        try{
            products.forEach(function(element) {
                piwikAddEcommerceItem(element.id, element.name, element.category, element.price, element.quantity);
            });
            piwikTrackEcommerceOrder(orderId);
        }
        catch(error) {}
    };

    var trackEcommercePromoImpression = function(id, name, creative, position){
        pushGTMDataLayer({
            'event': 'hktvEcomSliderImpression',
            'virtualPage': creative + position,
            'ecommerce': {
                'promoView': {
                    'promotions': [{
                        'id': id,
                        'name': name,
                        'creative': creative,
                        'position': position
                    }]
                }
            }
        });
	};
	
	var trackEcommercePromoImpressionMulti = function(array){
		if(array && array.length > 0){
			pushGTMDataLayer({
				'event': 'hktvEcomSliderImpression',
				'virtualPage': array[0]['creative'] + array[0]['position'],
				'ecommerce': {
					'promoView': {
						'promotions': array
					}
				}
			});
		}
    };

    var trackEcommercePromoClick = function(id, name, creative, position){
        pushGTMDataLayer({
            'event': 'hktvEcomSliderClick',
            'ecommerce': {
                'promoClick': {
                    'promotions': [{
                        'id': id,
                        'name': name,
                        'creative': creative,
                        'position': position
                    }]
                }
            },
            'eventCallback': function() {
                //document.location = promoObj.destinationUrl;
            }
        });
    };

    var trackLandingPage = function(landing){
        var landing = landing || '';
        pushGTMDataLayer({
            'landing' : landing
        });
        trackGTMCustomEvent('LandingPage');
        trackPage();
    };

    var trackLogin = function(){
        trackGTMCustomEvent('Login');
    };

    var trackRegisterSuccess = function(gender, ageRange, incomeRange){
        //use InappCommunicationManager for inapp webview
        if (webType == 'mobile' && isInApp){
            var registerParams = {
                "gender": gender || '',
                "ageRange": ageRange || '',
                "incomeRange": incomeRange || ''
            };
            InappCommunicationManager.sendAnalytics(inappAnalyticsNamespace.registerSuccess, registerParams);

        } else {
            pushGTMDataLayer({
                'user': {
                    'gender': gender || '',
                    'ageRange': ageRange || '',
                    'incomeRange': incomeRange || ''
                }
            });
            trackGTMCustomEvent('RegisterSuccess');
        }
    };

    var trackEcommercePDP = function(productName, productCode, price, productBrand, catCode, storeCode){

        var trimmedPrice = trimDisplayPrice(price) || '';

        pushGTMDataLayer({
            'event': 'hktvEcomPDP',
            'ecommerce': {
                'detail': {
                    'products': [{
                        'name': productName,
                        'id': productCode,
                        'price': trimmedPrice,
                        'brand': productBrand,
                        'category': catCode,
                        'variant': '',
                        'dimension2': storeCode
                    }]
                }
            }
        });
    };

    var trackProductDetailPage = function(productCode, baseProductCode, storeCode, catCode){
        pushGTMDataLayer({
            google_tag_params : {
                ecomm_category: catCode,
                ecomm_prodid: productCode,
                ecomm_pagetype: "product"
            },
            'Category': catCode,
            'SKU': productCode,
            'SKU_base': baseProductCode,
            'Store':storeCode
        });
        trackGTMCustomEvent('ProductDetailPage');

        try{
            piwikTrackPage();
        }
        catch(error) {}
        return true;
    };

    var trackSearchResultPage = function(analyticsObj){
        if (analyticsObj)
            pushGTMDataLayer({
                'keyword': analyticsObj.keyword || '',
                'Category': analyticsObj.Category || '',
                'landing': analyticsObj.landing || ''
            });
        trackGTMCustomEvent('SearchResultPage');
        trackPage();
    };

    var trackEcommerceAddToCart = function(productName, productCode, price, productBrand, catCode, quantity, storeCode){

        var trimmedPrice = trimDisplayPrice(price) || '';

        pushGTMDataLayer({
            'event': 'hktvEcommAddToCart',
            'ecommerce': {
                'currencyCode': 'HKD',
                'add': {
                    'products': [{
                        'name': productName,
                        'id': productCode,
                        'price': trimmedPrice,
                        'brand': productBrand,
                        'category': catCode,
                        'variant': '',
                        'quantity': quantity,
                        'dimension2': storeCode
                    }]
                }
            }
        });
    };

    var trackEcommerceRemoveFromCart = function(productName, productCode, price, productBrand, catCode, quantity, storeCode){

        var trimmedPrice = trimDisplayPrice(price) || '';

        pushGTMDataLayer({
            'event': 'hktvEcommRemoveFromCart',
            'ecommerce': {
                'remove': {
                    'products': [{
                        'name': productName,
                        'id': productCode,
                        'price': trimmedPrice,
                        'brand': productBrand,
                        'category': catCode,
                        'variant': '',
                        'quantity': quantity,
                        'dimension2': storeCode
                    }]
                }
            }
        });
    };

    var trackAddToCart = function(productCode, baseProductCode, storeCode, catCode, quantity){
        pushGTMDataLayer({
            google_tag_params : {
                ecomm_category: catCode,
                ecomm_prodid: productCode,
                ecomm_pagetype: "product"
            },
            'Category': catCode,
            'SKU': productCode,
            'SKU_base': baseProductCode,
            'Store':storeCode,
            'quantity':quantity
        });
        trackGTMCustomEvent('AddToCart');
    };
    var trackCartPage = function(deliveryEntries, enhancedEcom){
        var products = [];
        var deliveryEntries = deliveryEntries || [];
        var productPrice;
        var displayUnitPrice;
        var trimmedDisplayUnitPrice;
        var enhancedEcom = enhancedEcom || false;

        for (var i in deliveryEntries) {
            var orderEntries = deliveryEntries[i].orderEntries || deliveryEntries[i].entries || [];

            for (var j in orderEntries) {
                var orderEntry = orderEntries[j];

                productPrice = 0;
                for(var k in orderEntry.product.priceList){
                    productPrice = orderEntry.product.priceList[k].value;
                    if(orderEntry.product.priceList[k].priceType == 'DISCOUNT') {
                        break;
                    }
                }

                displayUnitPrice = orderEntry.discountedUnitPrice.formattedValue || 0;
                trimmedDisplayUnitPrice = trimDisplayPrice(displayUnitPrice) || '';

                if(enhancedEcom == true){
                    products.push({
                        'name': orderEntry.product.name || '',
                        'id': orderEntry.product.code || '',
                        'price': trimmedDisplayUnitPrice,
                        'brand': orderEntry.product.brandName || '',
                        'category': orderEntry.product.primaryCatCode || '',
                        'variant': '',
                        'quantity': orderEntry.quantity || 0,
                        'dimension2': orderEntry.product.storeCode || ''
                    });
                }else{
                    products.push({
                        'name': orderEntry.product.name || '',
                        'id': orderEntry.product.code || '',
                        'baseProduct': orderEntry.product.baseProduct || '',
                        'price': productPrice,
                        'brand': orderEntry.product.brandName || '',
                        'category': orderEntry.product.primaryCatCode || '',
                        'variant': '',
                        'quantity': orderEntry.quantity || 0,
                        'coupon': ''
                    });
                }

            }
        }

        if(enhancedEcom == true){
            pushGTMDataLayer({
                'event': 'hktvEcommInitCart',
                'ecommerce': {
                    'checkout': {
                        'actionField': {'step': 1},
                        'products': products
                    }
                }
            });
        }else{
            pushGTMDataLayer({  // send null to clear the cart first
                'cart':null
            });
            pushGTMDataLayer({
                'cart':products
            });
            trackGTMCustomEvent('Purchase');
        }
    };

    var trackGoToChekcout = function(deliveryEntries){
        var products = [];
        var deliveryEntries = deliveryEntries || [];
        var productPrice;
        var displayUnitPrice;
        var trimmedDisplayUnitPrice;

        for (var i in deliveryEntries) {
            var orderEntries = deliveryEntries[i].orderEntries || deliveryEntries[i].entries || [];

            for (var j in orderEntries) {
                var orderEntry = orderEntries[j];

                productPrice = 0;
                for(var k in orderEntry.product.priceList){
                    productPrice = orderEntry.product.priceList[k].value;
                    if(orderEntry.product.priceList[k].priceType == 'DISCOUNT') {
                        break;
                    }
                }

             displayUnitPrice = orderEntry.discountedUnitPrice.formattedValue || 0;
                trimmedDisplayUnitPrice = trimDisplayPrice(displayUnitPrice) || '';

                products.push({
                    'name': orderEntry.product.name || '',
                    'id': orderEntry.product.code || '',
                    'price': trimmedDisplayUnitPrice,
                    'brand': orderEntry.product.brandName || '',
                    'category': orderEntry.product.primaryCatCode || '',
                    'variant': '',
                    'quantity': orderEntry.quantity || 0,
                    'dimension2': orderEntry.product.storeCode || ''
                });
            }
        }

        pushGTMDataLayer({
            'event': 'hktvEcommGoToChekcout',
            'ecommerce': {
                'checkout': {
                    'actionField': {'step': 2},
                    'products': products
                }
            }
        });
    };

    var trackPurchase = function(deliveryEntries, step){
        //ecommerce
        var products = [];
        var deliveryEntries = deliveryEntries || [];
        var productPrice;
        var displayUnitPrice;
        var trimmedDisplayUnitPrice;
        var step = step || '3';
        var ids = [], brands = [], categories = [], names = [], quantities = [], prices =[], variants = [], storeCodes = [];

        for (var i in deliveryEntries) {
            var orderEntries = deliveryEntries[i].orderEntries || deliveryEntries[i].entries || [];

            for (var j in orderEntries) {
                var orderEntry = orderEntries[j];

                productPrice = 0;
                for(var k in orderEntry.product.priceList){
                    productPrice = orderEntry.product.priceList[k].value;
                    if(orderEntry.product.priceList[k].priceType == 'DISCOUNT') {
                        break;
                    }
                }


                displayUnitPrice = orderEntry.discountedUnitPrice.formattedValue || 0;
                trimmedDisplayUnitPrice = trimDisplayPrice(displayUnitPrice) || '';

                products.push({
                    'name': orderEntry.product.name || '',
                    'id': orderEntry.product.code || '',
                    'price': trimmedDisplayUnitPrice,
                    'brand': orderEntry.product.brandName || '',
                    'category': orderEntry.product.primaryCatCode || '',
                    'variant': '',
                    'quantity': orderEntry.quantity || 0,
                    'storeCode': orderEntry.product.storeCode || ''
                });
            }
        }
        for(var i in products){ // product array for inapp tunnelling
            var product = products[i] || {};
            ids.push(product.id);
            brands.push(product.brand);
            categories.push(product.category);
            names.push(product.name);
            quantities.push(product.quantity);
            prices.push(product.price);
            storeCodes.push(product.storeCode);
        }

        if (webType == 'mobile' && isInApp){
            var checkoutParams = {
                'p': ids,
                'pName': names,
                'pPrice': prices,
                'pBrand': brands,
                'pCat': categories,
                'pVariant': '',
                'pQty': quantities,
                'pStore': storeCodes
            };
            InappCommunicationManager.sendAnalytics(inappAnalyticsNamespace.initiateCheckout, checkoutParams);
        }else{
            pushGTMDataLayer({
                'event': 'hktvEcommProceedToPayment',
                'ecommerce': {
                    'checkout': {
                        'actionField': {'step': step},
                        'products': products
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    };

    var trackTransaction = function(orderObj, siteName, transactionFailed){
        if(typeof orderObj == 'undefined') return;

        var ids = [], baseIds = [], categories = [], names = [], quantities = [], prices =[], couponIds = [], storeCodes = [];
        var orderId = orderObj.code || '';
        var orderAmount = orderObj.totalPrice.value || 0;
        var orderEntries = orderObj.entries || [];
        var displayUnitPrice;
        var trimmedDisplayUnitPrice;

        if (typeof orderObj.appliedVouchers != 'undefined'){
            var voucher;
            for (var i in orderObj.appliedVouchers){
                voucher = orderObj.appliedVouchers[i];
                couponIds.push(voucher.voucherCode || '');
            }
        }

        var products_ga = [], products = [], productPrice;
        for(var i in orderEntries){
            var orderEntry = orderEntries[i];
            productPrice = 0;
            for(var j in orderEntries[i].product.priceList){
                productPrice = orderEntries[i].product.priceList[j].value;
                if(orderEntries[i].product.priceList[j].priceType == 'DISCOUNT') {
                    break;
                }
            }

            displayUnitPrice = orderEntry.discountedUnitPrice.formattedValue || 0;
            trimmedDisplayUnitPrice = trimDisplayPrice(displayUnitPrice) || '';

            products_ga.push({ // exclusive for gtm enhanced ecommerce requirement
                'name': orderEntries[i].product.name || '',
                'id': orderEntries[i].product.code || '',
                'price': trimmedDisplayUnitPrice,
                'brand': orderEntries[i].product.brandName || '',
                'category': orderEntries[i].product.primaryCatCode || '',
                'variant': '',
                'quantity': orderEntries[i].quantity || 0,
                'coupon': '',
                'storeCode': orderEntries[i].product.storeCode || '',
            });
            products.push({ // for gtm datalayer
                'name': orderEntries[i].product.name || '',
                'id': orderEntries[i].product.code || '',
                'baseProduct': orderEntries[i].product.baseProduct || '',
                'price': trimmedDisplayUnitPrice,
                'brand': orderEntries[i].product.brandName || '',
                'category': orderEntries[i].product.primaryCatCode || '',
                'variant': '',
                'quantity': orderEntries[i].quantity || 0,
                'coupon': '',
                'storeCode': orderEntries[i].product.storeCode || '',
            });
        }

        for(var i in products){ // product array for inapp tunnelling
            var product = products[i] || {};
            ids.push(product.id);
            baseIds.push(product.baseProduct);
            categories.push(product.category);
            names.push(product.name);
            quantities.push(product.quantity);
            prices.push(product.price);
            storeCodes.push(product.storeCode);
        }

        //use InappCommunicationManager for inapp webview
        if (webType == 'mobile' && isInApp){
            var checkoutParams = {
                "orderNumber": orderId,
                "orderAmount": orderAmount,
                "orderCouponIds": couponIds,
                "p": ids,
                "pBase": baseIds,
                "pCat": categories,
                "pName": names,
                "pQty": quantities,
                "pPrice": prices,
                'pStore': storeCodes
            };

            if (transactionFailed == true) {
                InappCommunicationManager.sendAnalytics(inappAnalyticsNamespace.checkoutFail, checkoutParams);
            }
            else {
                InappCommunicationManager.sendAnalytics(inappAnalyticsNamespace.checkoutSuccess, checkoutParams);
            }
        }
        else{
            if (transactionFailed == true) {
                trackPage('/_ga/pageview/order_confirmation/fail/' + orderId);
                trackGTMCustomEvent('transactionFail');
            }
            else {
                
                fbq('track', 'Purchase', {
                    content_ids: ids,
                    content_type: 'product',
                    content_categories: categories,
                    num_items: quantities,
                    value: 0,
                    currency: 'USD',
                    order_id: orderId
                });
                

                if(localStorage.GA_lastOrderConfirmation != orderId) {
                    trackEcommerceOrder(orderId, siteName, products_ga);
                    trackPage('/_ga/pageview/order_confirmation/success/' + orderId);
                    pushGTMDataLayer({
                        'orderId' : orderId,
                        'orderAmount': orderAmount,
                        'couponId': couponIds,
                        'cart' : products
                    });
                    trackGTMCustomEvent('transactionSuccess');
                    localStorage.GA_lastOrderConfirmation = orderId;
                }
            }
        }
    };

    var trimDisplayPrice = function(formattedValue){
        // return "0.00" for zeroPrice, return trimmed price with digit and "."
        var formattedValue = formattedValue || '';
        var trimmedValue = '0.00';
        if(formattedValue.match(/\d|\./g)){
            trimmedValue =  formattedValue.replace(/[^\d\.]*/g, '');
        }
        return trimmedValue;
    };

    return {
        trackPage:trackPage,
        trackEvent:trackEvent,
		trackEcommercePromoImpression : trackEcommercePromoImpression,
		trackEcommercePromoImpressionMulti : trackEcommercePromoImpressionMulti,
        trackEcommercePromoClick : trackEcommercePromoClick,

        trackLogin : trackLogin,
        trackRegisterSuccess : trackRegisterSuccess,

        trackLandingPage : trackLandingPage,
        trackEcommercePDP : trackEcommercePDP,
        trackProductDetailPage : trackProductDetailPage,
        trackSearchResultPage : trackSearchResultPage,

        trackEcommerceAddToCart : trackEcommerceAddToCart,
        trackEcommerceRemoveFromCart : trackEcommerceRemoveFromCart,
        trackAddToCart : trackAddToCart,
        trackCartPage: trackCartPage,
        trackGoToChekcout: trackGoToChekcout,
        trackPurchase : trackPurchase,
        trackTransaction : trackTransaction,
        trimDisplayPrice : trimDisplayPrice
    };
})();


function GA_trackPage(pageUrl) {
    return analytics.trackPage(pageUrl);
}
function GA_trackEvent(category, action, opt_label, nonInteraction) {
    return analytics.trackEvent(category, action, opt_label, nonInteraction);
}
</script><script type="text/javascript" src="//www.googleadservices.com/pagead/conversion_async.js" async charset="utf-8"></script>

<script>
    (function(window, document){
        var key = "Supermarket-sliderIndex";
        var storageAvailable = function(type){
            //https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Web_Storage_API/Using_the_Web_Storage_API
            try {
                var storage = window[type],
                        x = '__storage_test__';
                storage.setItem(x, x);
                storage.removeItem(x);
                return true;
            }
            catch(e) {
                return false;
            }
        };


        var slider = document.querySelectorAll('.rotating-image-slider');

        if (slider.length > 0){
            var indexs = [];
            if (storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                if (localStorage[key]!=undefined){
                    indexs = localStorage[key].split(',');
                }
            }
            for (var i=0; i<slider.length; i++){
                var el = slider[i];

                var images= el.querySelectorAll(".image-wrapper");
                if ( images.length > 0 ){
                    var navBtn = el.querySelectorAll(".nav-btn");
                    var index = (indexs[i]==undefined||indexs[i]==""||indexs[i]==null)?0:parseInt(indexs[i])+1;
                    if (images.length <= index || isNaN(index)) {
                        index = 0;
                    }
                    indexs[i] = index;
                    images[index].className += "active";

                
                    images[index].className += " shown";
                    analytics.trackEcommercePromoImpression(
                        undefined,
                        images[index].querySelectorAll("a")[0].getAttribute('href'),
                        'Supermarket_Slider',
                        'Supermarket_Slider_'+images[index].querySelectorAll("a")[0].getAttribute('data-position')
                    );
                

                    navBtn[index].className += "active";
                }

            }
            if (storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                localStorage[key] = indexs;
            }
        }

    })(window, document);
</script>

    <script>
        
        function registerColorbox() {
            ColorboxDesktop.showIFrame(window.location.protocol + '//' + window.location.host + '/hktv/zh/register', {
                "width": 542,
                "height": 342,
            });
        }

        
        window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessage, false);
        function receiveMessage(event) {
            if (event.origin.indexOf(window.location.host) == -1)
                return;
            if ( typeof event.data == "string")
            {
                if (event.data.indexOf('resize') != -1) {
                    var elements = event.data.split(':');
                    ColorboxDesktop.resize({height: elements[1]});
                }
                else{
                    switch(event.data){
                        case 'reload_email':
                        case 'reload_facebook':
                            var sPageURL = parent.location.search.substring(1);
                            var sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&');
                            var reloadFlag = true;
                            var newSearch = '';
                            var platform = event.data.split('_')[1];
                            for (var i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++) {
                                if (i > 0)
                                    newSearch += '&';

                                var sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');
                                if (sParameterName[0] == 'register' && sParameterName[1] == 'true') {
                                    sParameterName[1] = 'false';
                                    reloadFlag = false;
                                }
                                newSearch += sParameterName[0] + '=' + sParameterName[1];
                            }

                            analytics.trackPage('/zh/Web/Registration/Success/'+platform);
                            try {
                                sessionStorage.registerSuccess = "true";
                            }catch(e){
                                console.log('storage not support');
                            }

                            if (reloadFlag) {
                                location.reload(true);
                            }
                            else {
                                location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + location.pathname + '?' + newSearch);
                            }

                            break;
                        case 'loadLoginPage':
                            if (typeof hktvCommon !== "undefined" && typeof hktvCommon.addPrefixToHktvUrl !== "undefined") {
                                location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + hktvCommon.addPrefixToHktvUrl("/login"));
                            }
                            break;
                        case 'loadForgotPasswordPage':
                            if (typeof hktvCommon !== "undefined" && typeof hktvCommon.addPrefixToHktvUrl !== "undefined") {
                                location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + hktvCommon.addPrefixToHktvUrl("/login/pw/request"));
                            }
                            break;
                        case 'loginSuccess':
                            location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + location.pathname + '?register=false');
                            break;
                        case 'snsLinkUpdated':
                            location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + hktvCommon.addPrefixToHktvUrl("/my-account?snsRedirect=linkAutoFailure"));
                            break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    </script>
    <script>
        //Load logos in cat menu if specified lazy load.
        
        (function lazyLoadCatLogos() {
            function run() {
                $(".navi .cat-menu").off("mouseover.catMenuLazyload");
                $(".navi .cat-menu img[data-src]").each(function (index, img) {
                    $(img).attr("src", $(img).data("src"));
                });
            }

            //Trigger onload.
            if (typeof window.onpageshow !== "undefined") {
                window.addEventListener("pageshow", function () {
                    window.setTimeout(function() {run()}, 30000);
                });
            }
            else {
                window.addEventListener("load", function () {
                    window.setTimeout(function() {run()}, 30000);
                });
            }
            
            //Trigger on hover catMenu.
            $(".navi .cat-menu").on("mouseover.catMenuLazyload", function (evt) {
                run();
            });
        })();

        
        $(document).ready(function(){
            // setup menu
            var $menu = $("#subnav>ul");
            var $masterMenu = $("#master-nav>ul");

            // jQuery-menu-aim: <meaningful part of the example>
            // Hook up events to be fired on menu row activation.
            $menu.menuAim({
                activate: activateSubmenu,
                deactivate: deactivateSubmenu,
                exitMenu: function(){return true;}
            });

            $masterMenu.menuAim({
                activate: activateSubmenu,
                deactivate: deactivateSubmenu,
                exitMenu: function(){return true;}
            });

            // jQuery-menu-aim: </meaningful part of the example>

            // jQuery-menu-aim: the following JS is used to show and hide the submenu
            // contents. Again, this can be done in any number of ways. jQuery-menu-aim
            // doesn't care how you do this, it just fires the activate and deactivate
            // events at the right times so you know when to show and hide your submenus.
            function activateSubmenu(row) {
                var $row = $(row),
                        $submenu = $(".submenu", row),
                        $subMasterMenu = $(".subnav", row);

                // Show the submenu
                if ($subMasterMenu.length>0){
                    $subMasterMenu.addClass("active");
                }else{
                    $submenu.addClass("active");
                }
                // Keep the currently activated row's highlighted look
                $row.find("a").addClass("maintainHover");
            }

            function deactivateSubmenu(row) {
                var $row = $(row),
                        $submenu = $(".submenu", row),
                        $subMasterMenu = $(".subnav", row);

                // Hide the submenu and remove the row's highlighted look
                if ($subMasterMenu.length>0){
                    $subMasterMenu.removeClass("active");
                }else{
                    $submenu.removeClass("active");
                }
                $row.find("a").removeClass("maintainHover");
            }

            // setup Header
			$(document).on('click.headerList', function(e) {
			    
			    if($(e.target).parents('.mymessage').length > 0) {
			        return;
			    }

				$("#header .btn-mylist, #header .btn-msgCenter, #header .btn-myaccount").each(function(){
					if (!$(this).hasClass('show')) {
				    	$(this).siblings('.list').hide();
				    	$(this).removeClass('active');
					}
					$(this).siblings('.list').children("li").show();
					$(this).removeClass('show');
				});
			});
			$("#header .btn-mylist, #header .btn-msgCenter, #header .btn-myaccount").on('click.headerList', function (e) {
			    if (!$(this).siblings('.list').is(':visible')) {
				    $(this).siblings('.list').show();
			    	$(this).addClass('active').addClass('show');
                    
			    }
			});
			if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
				if (localStorage.myaccountLastAutoOpen) {
					var oldDate = new Date(parseInt(localStorage.myaccountLastAutoOpen));
					var currentDate = new Date();

					var oldDay = new Date(oldDate.getFullYear(), oldDate.getMonth(), oldDate.getDate());
					var currentDay = new Date(currentDate.getFullYear(), currentDate.getMonth(), currentDate.getDate());

					var ms = Math.abs(currentDay-oldDay);
					var dayDiff = Math.floor(ms/1000/60/60/24);
					if(dayDiff > 0) {
						// show
						localStorage.myaccountLastAutoOpen = currentDate.getTime();
						$("#header .btn-myaccount").trigger('click.headerList').siblings('.list').children("li:nth-child(n+2)").hide();
					}
				} else {
					localStorage.myaccountLastAutoOpen = new Date().getTime();
					$("#header .btn-myaccount").trigger('click.headerList').siblings('.list').children("li:nth-child(n+2)").hide();
				}
			}
            
            stickyHeaderLastStatus = "";
            function stickTop() {
                fastdom.measure(function(){

                    var docW = window.innerWidth;
                    var docH = window.innerHeight;
                    var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
                    var headerHiddenHeight = $("#header .top").outerHeight() + $("#header .banner-1188").outerHeight();

                    if (docW > 1208) {
                        if (docH <= 600) {
                            headerHiddenHeight += $("#header #tab").outerHeight();
                        }

                        $("#header").removeClass("hidden-header");
                        if (scrollTop>headerHiddenHeight){
                            var mainWrapperPaddingHeight = $("#header").outerHeight();
                            if (docH > 600){
                                if (stickyHeaderLastStatus != 'fullStickyHeader'){
                                    stickyHeaderLastStatus = 'fullStickyHeader';
                                    $(document).trigger(stickyHeaderLastStatus);
                                }
                            }else{
                                if (stickyHeaderLastStatus != 'halfStickyHeader'){
                                    stickyHeaderLastStatus = 'halfStickyHeader';
                                    $(document).trigger(stickyHeaderLastStatus);
                                }
                            }
                            fastdom.mutate(function(){
                                $("#tab li").addClass("small-tab");
                                $("#header").css("top", "-"+headerHiddenHeight+"px");
                                $("#mainWrapper").css("padding-top", mainWrapperPaddingHeight+"px");
                                $("#header").addClass("sticky-header");
                                $(".cat-menu>#subnav").addClass("subnav-off");


                                if ( window.bannerTopEnabled) {
                                    var $bannerTop = $('#bannerTop');
                                    if ($bannerTop.length > 0 && typeof $bannerTop.data('bannerTop') == 'object') $bannerTop.data('bannerTop').closeBannerTopOverlay();
                                }

                            });

                        }else{
                            fastdom.mutate(function() {
                                $("#header").removeClass("sticky-header");
                                $("#tab li").removeClass("small-tab");

                                $("#header").css("top", 0+"px");
                                $("#mainWrapper").css("padding-top", 0+"px");

                                $(".cat-menu>#subnav").removeClass("subnav-off");


                                if ( window.bannerTopEnabled) {
                                    var $bannerTop = $('#bannerTop');
                                    if ($bannerTop.length > 0 && typeof $bannerTop.data('bannerTop') == 'object') $bannerTop.data('bannerTop').openBannerTopOverlay();
                                }
                            });

                            if (stickyHeaderLastStatus != 'noneStickyHeader'){
                                stickyHeaderLastStatus = 'noneStickyHeader';
                                $(document).trigger(stickyHeaderLastStatus);
                            }

                        }
                    } else {
                        if (stickyHeaderLastStatus != 'hiddenHeader'){
                            stickyHeaderLastStatus = 'hiddenHeader';
                            $(document).trigger(stickyHeaderLastStatus);
                        }

                        fastdom.mutate(function() {
                            $("#header").removeClass("sticky-header");
                            $("#header").css("top", 0+"px");
                            $("#mainWrapper").css("padding-top", 0+"px");

                        });

                        if ( window.bannerTopEnabled) {
                            var $bannerTop = $('#bannerTop');
                            if ($bannerTop.length > 0 && typeof $bannerTop.data('bannerTop') == 'object'){

                                if (scrollTop > ($("#header .banner-1188").outerHeight() || 100)){
                                    $bannerTop.data('bannerTop').closeBannerTopOverlay();
                                } else {
                                    $bannerTop.data('bannerTop').openBannerTopOverlay();
                                }

                            }

                        }
                    }
                });
            }

            window.addEventListener('scroll', function(){
                stickTop();
                CrazyAd();
            });
            window.addEventListener('resize', function(){
                stickTop();
                CrazyAd();
            });

            var sPageURL = window.location.search.substring(1);
            var sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&');
            for (var i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++)
            {
                var sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');
                if (sParameterName[0] == 'register' && sParameterName[1]=='true')
                {
                    $('.btn-register').click();
                }
            }
        });
        
        //Scroll left and right
        function CrazyAd() {
            fastdom.measure(function(){
                var sl = window.scrollX;
                if (sl > 0 ) {
                    fastdom.mutate(function(){
                        var $CrazyAd = $(".CrazyAd");
                        $CrazyAd.css({
                            "left": -sl + "px"
                        });
                    });
                }
            });
        }

            lang: {
                between: '在',
                category: '分類',
                storetitle: '瀏覽商店'
            }
        });

        
        function applyCheckoutRestrictions(e){
            if (e.currentTarget.dataset['restricted'] != undefined && e.currentTarget.dataset['restricted']=='false'){
                e.currentTarget.dataset['restricted'] = "true";
            }else {
                e.preventDefault();
            }
        }

    $("body").on("autoFillCompleted", function(){
        $("body").off("autoFillCompleted");
        // if nothing, do not add listener
        if ($(".extra-banner-container img").length>0){
            // on close handling
            $(".extra-banner-container .closeBtn").on("click", function(){
                //set cookie and wait for 20mins.
                if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                    if (!Date.now) {
                        Date.now = function() { return new Date().getTime(); }
                    }
                    localStorage.bannerExpiry = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
                }
                $(".extra-banner-container").removeClass("active").remove();
            });
            // onscroll handling
            var shouldShow = true;
            if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                if (!Date.now) {
                    Date.now = function() { return new Date().getTime(); }
                }
                if (localStorage.bannerExpiry){
                    if (Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) < parseInt(localStorage.bannerExpiry)+1200){
                        shouldShow = false;
                    }else{
                        localStorage.removeItem("bannerExpiry");
                    }
                }
            }
            if (shouldShow){
                $(window).scroll(function(e){
                    var height = 99;

                    fastdom.measure(function() {
                        var h = window.scrollY;
                        // if h > height, show else hidden
                        fastdom.mutate(function(){
                            if (h > height){
                                $(".extra-banner-container").addClass("active");
                            }else{
                                $(".extra-banner-container").removeClass("active");
                            }
                        });
                    });

                });
            }

        }
        //only for crazy ad
        if ($(".CrazyAd-container img").length>0){
            // on close handling
            $(".CrazyAd-container .btnCloseLarge").on("click", function(){
                //set localstorage
                if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                    if (!Date.now) {
                        Date.now = function() { return new Date().getTime(); }
                    }
                    localStorage.CrazyAdbannerExpiry = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
                }
                $(".CrazyAd").hide();
            });
            $(".CrazyAd-container #topBannerImg").on("click", function(){
                //set localstorage
                if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                    if (!Date.now) {
                        Date.now = function() { return new Date().getTime(); }
                    }
                    localStorage.CrazyAdbannerExpiry = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
                }
                $(".CrazyAd").hide();
            });

            var shouldShow = true;
            if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                if (!Date.now) {
                    Date.now = function() { return new Date().getTime(); }
                }
                if (localStorage.CrazyAdbannerExpiry){
                    // wait for 20mins
                    if (Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) < parseInt(localStorage.CrazyAdbannerExpiry)+1200){
                        shouldShow = false;

                    }else{
                        localStorage.removeItem("CrazyAdbannerExpiry");
                    }

                }
            }
            if (shouldShow){
               $(".CrazyAd").show();
            }
            else {
               $(".CrazyAd").hide();
            }

        }
});

        lookup: false,
        zones: ["SLA", "SLB", "SLC", "SLD","CRA"],
        categories: ['supermarket'],
        lang: "zh",
        autoFill: true

<script>
    (function($, window, document){

        (function(f) {
            window.setSliderTimeout = f(window.setTimeout);   // extends the global function!
            window.setSliderInterval = f(window.setInterval); // extends the global function!
        })(function(f) {
            return function(c, t) {
                var a = [].slice.call(arguments, 2);    // gathers the extra args
                return f(function() {
                    c.apply(this, a);                   // passes them to your function
                }, t);
            };
        });

        
        var slider = $(".rotating-image-slider");
        var navBtnGlobal = $(".nav-btn", slider);
        var timeoutIDs = [];
        var indexs = [];
        var key = "Supermarket-sliderIndex";

        function slideInit(i) {
            if (i!=undefined){
                timeoutIDs[i] = setSliderTimeout(animateSlide, 5000, i);
            }else{
                if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                    if (localStorage[key]!=undefined){
                        indexs = localStorage[key].split(',');
                    }
                }
                slider.each(function(j){
                    // define which banner should be active is done by inline js
                    // we set the timer only in here
                    timeoutIDs.push(setSliderTimeout(animateSlide, 5000, j));
                });
            }
        }
        function animateSlide(j) {
            var images=$(".image-wrapper", slider[j]);
            if (images.length>1){
                images.each(function(index){
                    if ($(this).hasClass("active")){
                        $(this).removeClass("active");
                        var navBtn = $(".nav-btn", slider[j])
                        navBtn.eq(index).removeClass("active");
                        var nextIndex = (images.length>index+1)?index+1:0;
                        images.eq(nextIndex).addClass("active");

                        
                        if($(window).scrollTop() < (images.offset().top + images.height()) && !images.eq(nextIndex).hasClass("shown")){
                            images.eq(nextIndex).addClass("shown");
                            // TODO : trigger impression
                            analytics.trackEcommercePromoImpression(
                                undefined,
                                $(images).eq(nextIndex).find('a').attr('href'),
                                'Supermarket_Slider',
                                'Supermarket_Slider_'+$(images).eq(nextIndex).find('a').data('position')
                            );
                        }
                        

                        navBtn.eq(nextIndex).addClass("active");
                        timeoutIDs[j]=(setSliderTimeout(animateSlide, 5000, j));

                        //update index
                        indexs[j] = nextIndex ;
                        if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                            localStorage[key] = indexs;
                        }


                        return false;
                    }
                });


            }

        }
        function clearAnimateSlide(i) {
            if (i!=undefined){
                window.clearTimeout(timeoutIDs[i]);
            }else{
                for (var id in timeoutIDs){
                    window.clearTimeout(timeoutIDs[id]);
                }
                timeoutIDs = [];
                indexs = [] ;
                if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                    localStorage.removeItem(key);
                }

            }
        }

        navBtnGlobal.on("click", function(){
            var index = $(this).data("index");
            var self = this;
            slider.each(function(i){
                if ($.contains(this, self)){
                    var images=$(".image-wrapper", this);
                    var navBtn = $(".nav-btn", this);
                    images.removeClass("active");
                    navBtn.removeClass("active");

                    //update index
                    indexs[i] = index ;
                    if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                        localStorage[key] = indexs;
                    }

                    images.eq(index).addClass("active");

                    
                    if(!images.eq(index).hasClass("shown")){
                        images.eq(index).addClass("shown");
                        analytics.trackEcommercePromoImpression(
                            undefined,
                            images.eq(index).find('a').attr('href'),
                            'Supermarket_Slider',
                            'Supermarket_Slider_'+images.eq(index).find('a').data('position')
                        );
                    }
                    

                    navBtn.eq(index).addClass("active");
                    clearAnimateSlide(i);
                    slideInit(i);
                }
            });
        });
        slideInit();
    })(jQuery, window, document);


</script>

        var url = $(this).attr("href");
        var name = "Supermarket_Top30_" + $(this).parents(".card").data("category") + "_PI_False";
        var creative = "Supermarket_Top30";
        var position = "Supermarket_Top30_" + $(this).parents(".card").data("position");

        analytics.trackEcommercePromoClick(url, name, creative, position);
    });

    function trackTop30Impression() {
        if ($("#hot-categories-fallback").length == 0 || $("#hot-categories-fallback").is(":visible")) {
            $('#top30-categories .card a:not(.impressed)').each(function (index, element) {
                var cardIsShown = !$(".top30CategoriesShowMoreButton").is(":visible") || index < 8;

                if (cardIsShown && $(element).componentInScreen()) {
                    var url = $(element).attr("href");
                    var name = "Supermarket_Top30_" + $(element).parents(".card").data("category") + "_PI_False";
                    var creative = "Supermarket_Top30";
                    var position = "Supermarket_Top30_" + $(element).parents(".card").data("position");

                    analytics.trackEcommercePromoImpression(url, name, creative, position);
                    $(element).addClass("impressed");
                }
            });
        }
    }

    trackTop30Impression();
    $(window).on("scroll", _.debounce(trackTop30Impression, 100));

    $("body").on('click','#cboxClose', function() {
        if($('#cboxLoadedContent .productQuickViewWrapper').length>0){
            analytics.trackEvent('Supermarket','Overlay_Product_Close','N/A');
        }
        else{
            try{
                if($('iframe.cboxIframe')[0].contentWindow){
                    
                    if($('iframe.cboxIframe')[0].contentWindow.location.pathname.match('snsTokenError')){
                        analytics.trackPage('/_ga/Web/click/facebook/fail/cancel');
                        analytics.trackEvent('Account_Registration','Cancel','Step_Facebook_Fail');
                    }
                    else if($('iframe.cboxIframe')[0].contentWindow.location.pathname.match('snsAgeNotEnough')){
                        analytics.trackPage('/_ga/Web/click/facebook/fail/age_cancel');
                        analytics.trackEvent('Account_Registration','Age_Cancel','Step_Facebook_Fail');
                    }
                    
                }
            }
            catch (e){
                console.log('This cbox does not contain any iFrame.');
            }
        }
    });

    <script>
        function getParameterByName(name){
            name = name.replace(/[\[]/,"\\\[").replace(/[\]]/,"\\\]");
            var regexS = "[\\?&]"+name+"=([^&#]*)";
            var regex = new RegExp( regexS );
            var results = regex.exec( window.location.href );
            if( results == null ){
                return "";
            } else{
                return decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
            }
        }

        $( window ).load(function() {
            var scrollDest = getParameterByName('scrollTo');
            if(scrollDest == "promoCat"){
                hktvCommon.scrollToElement($('#promoCat'));
            }
        });
    </script><input type="hidden" value="page-supermarketLanding" class="landingCurrentPage">
